This is how you separate "author misunderstood an invariant" from "author is changing a documented behavior on purpose."


4. Severity is exactly one of: `blocking`, `medium`, `low`, `nit`. Use `blocking` ONLY for issues that must be fixed before merge.
5. The Surveyed section is REQUIRED even if you have zero findings. A specialist that returns only "No findings" has failed to do its job. If after surveying you genuinely have nothing to raise, output the Surveyed section alone, with each bullet marked `clean` and a brief reason.
6. Be specific. Cite file paths and line numbers. Quote the problematic code in ≤2 lines when it clarifies. **Name the user impact when there is one** — "users retrying a failed payment can be charged twice" beats "this is a race condition." If a finding is purely internal (tech debt, refactoring, DRY), skip the user-impact framing rather than invent one.
7. Keep each finding under 120 words. No preamble, no conclusion, no verdict. The aggregator will assemble the final review.
8. **Remedy-cost framing.** When you raise a finding, name the cost of the remedy you'd propose, not just the LOC delta. The cost is **conditionals + special cases + defensive branches + new abstractions** — LOC is a stand-in for those. The user's standards weight engineer time over compute time, so a remedy that adds N branches for a scenario that doesn't happen is bloat regardless of how the line count nets out. **Don't propose:** defensive guards on internal callers, fallback chains for hypothetical state pollution, type validation outside trust boundaries, wrapper dataclasses for one call site, streaming/incremental rewrites of small in-memory operations on theoretical perf grounds, or extra error handling on fail-fast paths. The test for any edge-case handler: *does the edge case actually happen, or will it in the near future?* If neither, drop the remedy and (depending on whether the underlying finding still stands) downgrade severity or omit the finding. Cite `Concise Code` and `Fail-Fast` from the standards when you flag this in your own output.

**Your angle: Simplification, DRY, and code-quality smells.**

FIRST, read `.codex-scratch/prior-art.md`. That's the output of `kid` — a semantic-similarity search that identifies blocks in *this PR's diff* that resemble existing code in the repo. Kid is noisy — not every hit is a real DRY violation — but every strong hit (score ≥ 0.75) deserves either a concrete dismissal or a finding. Kid also has blind spots: it only covers Python and Swift, only scores blocks ≥ 3 added lines, and will miss intra-PR duplication (two *new* blocks that resemble each other, not old code). Those blind spots are YOURS to catch.

Scope:
- **Cross-repo duplication (kid hits)**: for each kid hit you keep, cite both the new block and the prior-art target, and propose the shared helper/base/decorator that should absorb both. For kid hits you dismiss, say why (different contract, unavoidable coincidence, etc.).
- **Intra-PR duplication**: the PR adds N near-identical blocks at once — three near-identical HTTP handlers, three copies of the same guard pattern, three parallel changes to three modules, three new routes with the same shape. That's a missing abstraction the author hasn't yet extracted. Kid will not catch this — you must survey the diff yourself for N-times-repeated structure.
- **Verbose implementations**: code doing in 30 lines what 5 would do. Conditional-chain simplifications, missing early-returns, collapsing defensive-coding-gone-wild into direct access. Cite the user's Fail-Fast / Concise-Code standards when they apply.
- **Missing abstractions**: repeated patterns (same JSON shape built three times, same validation copied across routes, same setup in six tests) that are begging for a helper.
- **Drive-by tidies missed**: this PR is already touching a file — were obvious tidies left on the table that the author could have taken on their way through? Two nearly-identical mocks that could collapse into a factory; an unused import; a chain of `if`/`elif` that wants a dispatch dict; a one-line comment restating a function name; a defensive `(x or {}).get(...)` where the seam guarantees `x`. Standard: "leave each file a little better than you found it" — fewer LOC, fewer conditionals, clearer seam assumptions, louder failure when violated. Severity: usually `low` or `nit` — note them, don't block.

Out of scope (other specialists own these — do NOT raise):
- **Simplest-shape-vs-spirit-of-ask** (overall design overshoot, public-surface simplification, decomposition, wrong-shape smells like regex on structured input): `shape` owns this. Even when a simplification thread leads you toward "the whole shape is wrong," stop and let `shape` raise it.
- **Stale callers / dead public symbols** (cross-symbol call-graph effects): `consumers` owns these. Raise dead code here only when it's intra-PR (a helper added in this PR with zero callers in the same diff). Unused imports and dead-on-touch local helpers are YOURS — they're file-local cleanups, not call-graph effects, and consumers's out-of-scope explicitly disclaims them.
- Security bugs, concurrency bugs, test coverage gaps, strategic/roadmap concerns.

Severity tuning: DRY findings are usually `medium` or `low`. Reserve `blocking` only for severe cases (e.g., the same 100-line handler authored five times in one PR, or introduced code that duplicates a well-established utility that's already sitting in the repo).

Look beyond the diff: grep the repo for existing utilities/base classes that the PR's new code should have reused.

+#!/usr/bin/env bash
+# Mount a Plow DMG and assert it has no custom volume icon (PLO-29 regression
+# guard) and that the volume name is "Plow". Detaches before exiting.
+set -euo pipefail
+
+usage() {
+  cat <<'EOF'
+Usage: plowd-verify-dmg [--dmg <path>]
+
+Mounts the given DMG, asserts the mounted volume is named "Plow" and has no
+.VolumeIcon.icns at its root, then detaches. Defaults to .build/Plow.dmg
+relative to the repo root.
+EOF
+}
+
+repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
+dmg_path="${repo_root}/.build/Plow.dmg"
+
+while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
+  case "$1" in
+    --dmg)
+      dmg_path="${2:-}"
+      shift 2
+      ;;
+    -h|--help)
+      usage
+      exit 0
+      ;;
+    *)
+      echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
+      usage >&2
+      exit 1
+      ;;
+  esac
+done
+
+if [[ "${dmg_path}" != /* ]]; then
+  dmg_path="${repo_root}/${dmg_path}"
+fi
+
+[[ -f "${dmg_path}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG not found: ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+# Refuse to run when a Plow volume is already mounted: the new mountpoint
+# would be "Plow 1" / "Plow 2" / ..., which would mask a real regression in
+# the volume-name assertion below.
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
+if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
+  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before verifying:" >&2
+  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
+  exit 1
+fi
+
+mounted_volume=""
+cleanup() {
+  local rc=$?
+  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
+    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
+      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
+      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
+      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
+      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
+        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
+        exit 1
+      fi
+    else
+      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
+      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
+    fi
+  fi
+  exit "${rc}"
+}
+trap cleanup EXIT
+
+attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${dmg_path}" -nobrowse -readonly)"
+mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"
+[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to mount ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+volume_name="$(basename "${mounted_volume}")"
+[[ "${volume_name}" == "Plow" ]] || { echo "error: mounted volume name is '${volume_name}', expected 'Plow'" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+[[ ! -e "${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns" ]] || {
+  echo "error: ${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns exists; PLO-29 regression: DMG ships a custom volume icon" >&2
+  exit 1
+}
+
+echo "ok: ${dmg_path} mounts as 'Plow' with no custom volume icon"

+@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
+def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_dmg_shipping_volume_icon(tmp_path):
+    """PLO-29 artifact-level guard. Catches the failure mode that
+    ``test_signed_package_script_builds_ulfo_dmg_without_staging_ds_store``
+    cannot: a regression that re-attaches the DMG post-``hdiutil create``
+    and re-stages a custom volume icon at the final-image stage. We build
+    three real DMGs with hdiutil and assert plowd-verify-dmg accepts the
+    clean one and rejects each regression shape.
+
+    plowd-verify-dmg is wired into plowd-beta-package-signed between staple
+    and S3 upload, so a rejection here aborts ``just release`` before any
+    artifact ships."""
+    # Refuse to run if a real Plow volume is already mounted: the script
+    # bails on that and our assertions would tag the wrong failure mode.
+    info = subprocess.run(
+        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
+    )
+    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
+        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
+
+    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
+    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
+    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
+
+    def make_dmg(dmg_path: Path, *, volname: str) -> None:
+        subprocess.run(
+            [
+                "hdiutil", "create",
+                "-volname", volname,
+                "-srcfolder", str(stage),
+                "-ov",
+                "-format", "ULFO",
+                str(dmg_path),
+            ],
+            check=True, capture_output=True,
+        )
+
+    def run_verify(dmg_path: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
+        return subprocess.run(
+            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg_path)],
+            capture_output=True, text=True,
+        )
+
+    # Happy path: clean Plow DMG with no .VolumeIcon must pass.
+    clean_dmg = tmp_path / "clean.dmg"
+    make_dmg(clean_dmg, volname="Plow")
+    ok = run_verify(clean_dmg)
+    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"clean DMG rejected: stdout={ok.stdout!r} stderr={ok.stderr!r}"
+
+    # Regression #1: someone re-introduces .VolumeIcon.icns at the volume root.
+    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_text("fake-icns")
+    iconed_dmg = tmp_path / "iconed.dmg"
+    make_dmg(iconed_dmg, volname="Plow")
+    fail = run_verify(iconed_dmg)
+    assert fail.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns"
+    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in fail.stderr
+
+    # Regression #2: someone parameterizes -volname to something other than "Plow".
+    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").unlink()
+    misnamed_dmg = tmp_path / "misnamed.dmg"
+    make_dmg(misnamed_dmg, volname="NotPlow")
+    fail2 = run_verify(misnamed_dmg)
+    assert fail2.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG with wrong volume name"
+    assert "expected 'Plow'" in fail2.stderr
+
+
+@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
+def test_plowd_verify_dmg_propagates_detach_failure_on_success_path(tmp_path):
+    """Round-2: if `hdiutil detach` fails on the success path (e.g. the
+    volume is busy), plowd-verify-dmg must exit non-zero. The previous
+    `|| true` swallowed the failure and returned 0, leaking /Volumes/Plow,
+    which then tripped ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume on the next release
+    retry. This test injects an `hdiutil` wrapper whose `detach` always
+    fails and asserts the script surfaces it."""
+    info = subprocess.run(
+        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
+    )
+    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
+        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
+
+    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
+    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
+    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
+    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
+    subprocess.run(
+        [
+            "hdiutil", "create",
+            "-volname", "Plow",
+            "-srcfolder", str(stage),
+            "-ov",
+            "-format", "ULFO",
+            str(dmg),
+        ],
+        check=True, capture_output=True,
+    )
+
+    real_hdiutil = subprocess.run(
+        ["which", "hdiutil"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
+    ).stdout.strip()
+    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
+    fake_bin.mkdir()
+    wrapper = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
+    wrapper.write_text(
+        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
+        f'if [[ "$1" == "detach" ]]; then\n'
+        f'  echo "fake: detach failure (test injection)" >&2\n'
+        f'  exit 16\n'
+        f'fi\n'
+        f'exec "{real_hdiutil}" "$@"\n'
+    )
+    wrapper.chmod(0o755)
+
+    try:
+        result = subprocess.run(
+            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg)],
+            capture_output=True, text=True,
+            env={
+                **subprocess.os.environ,
+                "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
+            },
+        )
+        assert result.returncode != 0, (
+            f"verify-dmg returned 0 despite detach failure; mount leaked.\n"
+            f"stdout={result.stdout!r}\nstderr={result.stderr!r}"
+        )
+        assert "failed to detach" in result.stderr, (
+            f"expected 'failed to detach' in stderr, got: {result.stderr!r}"
+        )
+    finally:
+        # Real hdiutil to clean up the leaked mount the wrapper refused to release.
+        subprocess.run(
+            [real_hdiutil, "detach", "/Volumes/Plow"],
+            capture_output=True,
+        )
+
+

     app_bundle = tmp_path / "Plow.app"
     output = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"

     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	# Mount a Plow DMG and assert it has no custom volume icon (PLO-29 regression
     3	# guard) and that the volume name is "Plow". Detaches before exiting.
     4	set -euo pipefail
     5	
     6	usage() {
     7	  cat <<'EOF'
     8	Usage: plowd-verify-dmg [--dmg <path>]
     9	
    10	Mounts the given DMG, asserts the mounted volume is named "Plow" and has no
    11	.VolumeIcon.icns at its root, then detaches. Defaults to .build/Plow.dmg
    12	relative to the repo root.
    13	EOF
    14	}
    15	
    16	repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
    17	dmg_path="${repo_root}/.build/Plow.dmg"
    18	
    19	while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
    20	  case "$1" in
    21	    --dmg)
    22	      dmg_path="${2:-}"
    23	      shift 2
    24	      ;;
    25	    -h|--help)
    26	      usage
    27	      exit 0
    28	      ;;
    29	    *)
    30	      echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
    31	      usage >&2
    32	      exit 1
    33	      ;;
    34	  esac
    35	done
    36	
    37	if [[ "${dmg_path}" != /* ]]; then
    38	  dmg_path="${repo_root}/${dmg_path}"
    39	fi
    40	
    41	[[ -f "${dmg_path}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG not found: ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
    42	
    43	# Refuse to run when a Plow volume is already mounted: the new mountpoint
    44	# would be "Plow 1" / "Plow 2" / ..., which would mask a real regression in
    45	# the volume-name assertion below.
    46	mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
    47	mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
    48	if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
    49	  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before verifying:" >&2
    50	  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
    51	  exit 1
    52	fi
    53	
    54	mounted_volume=""
    55	cleanup() {
    56	  local rc=$?
    57	  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
    58	    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
    59	      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
    60	      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
    61	      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
    62	      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
    63	        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
    64	        exit 1
    65	      fi
    66	    else
    67	      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
    68	      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    69	    fi
    70	  fi
    71	  exit "${rc}"
    72	}
    73	trap cleanup EXIT
    74	
    75	attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${dmg_path}" -nobrowse -readonly)"
    76	mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"
    77	[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to mount ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
    78	
    79	volume_name="$(basename "${mounted_volume}")"
    80	[[ "${volume_name}" == "Plow" ]] || { echo "error: mounted volume name is '${volume_name}', expected 'Plow'" >&2; exit 1; }
    81	
    82	[[ ! -e "${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns" ]] || {
    83	  echo "error: ${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns exists; PLO-29 regression: DMG ships a custom volume icon" >&2
    84	  exit 1
    85	}
    86	
    87	echo "ok: ${dmg_path} mounts as 'Plow' with no custom volume icon"

    13	VALIDATE_PACKAGE_SCRIPT = REPO_ROOT / "app" / "plowd" / "scripts" / "plowd-validate-package"

    19	
    20	def _provision_fake_bin(fake_bin: Path, systemctl_log: Path) -> None:
    21	    """Write stub commands sufficient to run provision-runtime.sh on macOS."""
    22	    stubs = {
    23	        # zstd just needs to be on PATH so the apt-get install branch is skipped
    24	        "zstd": "#!/bin/sh\n",
    25	        # sha256sum: hash stdin or file args, mimicking GNU coreutils behaviour
    26	        "sha256sum": textwrap.dedent("""\
    27	            #!/usr/bin/env python3
    28	            import hashlib, sys
    29	            from pathlib import Path
    30	            args = [a for a in sys.argv[1:] if a != "--"]
    31	            if args:
    32	                for arg in args:
    33	                    try:
    34	                        data = Path(arg).read_bytes()
    35	                        print(hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest() + "  " + arg)
    36	                    except FileNotFoundError:
    37	                        print(f"sha256sum: {arg}: No such file or directory", file=sys.stderr)
    38	                        sys.exit(1)
    39	            else:
    40	                data = sys.stdin.buffer.read()
    41	                print(hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest() + "  -")
    42	            """),
    43	        # systemctl: log every invocation; always succeed
    44	        "systemctl": f'#!/bin/sh\necho "$@" >> "{systemctl_log}"\n',
    45	    }
    46	    for name, body in stubs.items():
    47	        p = fake_bin / name
    48	        p.write_text(body)
    49	        p.chmod(0o755)
    50	
    51	
    52	def _run_provision(tmp_path: Path, fake_bin: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
    53	    unit_dir = tmp_path / "units"
    54	    unit_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    55	    libexec_dir = tmp_path / "libexec"
    56	    libexec_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    57	    return subprocess.run(
    58	        ["bash", str(PROVISION_SCRIPT)],
    59	        capture_output=True,
    60	        text=True,
    61	        env={
    62	            **subprocess.os.environ,
    63	            "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
    64	            "PLOW_UNIT_DIR": str(unit_dir),
    65	            "PLOW_LIBEXEC_DIR": str(libexec_dir),
    66	        },
    67	    )
    68	
    69	
    70	def test_provision_restarts_containerd_on_first_run(tmp_path):
    71	    """containerd.service is restarted when unit files are written for the first time."""
    72	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
    73	    fake_bin.mkdir()
    74	    systemctl_log = tmp_path / "systemctl.log"
    75	    _provision_fake_bin(fake_bin, systemctl_log)
    76	
    77	    result = _run_provision(tmp_path, fake_bin)
    78	    assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
    79	
    80	    calls = systemctl_log.read_text().splitlines()
    81	    assert any("restart containerd.service" in c for c in calls)
    82	
    83	
    84	def test_provision_skips_containerd_restart_when_units_unchanged(tmp_path):
    85	    """containerd.service is not restarted when provision writes identical unit files."""
    86	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
    87	    fake_bin.mkdir()
    88	    systemctl_log = tmp_path / "systemctl.log"
    89	    _provision_fake_bin(fake_bin, systemctl_log)
    90	
    91	    # First run — creates units from scratch; restart expected
    92	    r1 = _run_provision(tmp_path, fake_bin)
    93	    assert r1.returncode == 0, r1.stderr
    94	
    95	    # Second run — same unit content; containerd restart must be skipped
    96	    systemctl_log.unlink()
    97	    r2 = _run_provision(tmp_path, fake_bin)
    98	    assert r2.returncode == 0, r2.stderr
    99	
   100	    calls = systemctl_log.read_text().splitlines() if systemctl_log.exists() else []
   101	    assert not any("restart containerd.service" in c for c in calls), (
   102	        f"containerd was restarted on unchanged provision run:\n" + "\n".join(calls)
   103	    )
   104

   139	def test_git_ref_script_defaults_to_parent_commit_for_stable_rebuilds(tmp_path):
   140	    repo_root = tmp_path / "repo"
   141	    repo_root.mkdir()
   142	
   143	    def git(*args: str) -> str:
   144	        result = subprocess.run(
   145	            ["git", *args],
   146	            capture_output=True,
   147	            text=True,
   148	            cwd=repo_root,
   149	            check=True,
   150	        )
   151	        return result.stdout.strip()
   152	
   153	    git("init")
   154	    git("config", "user.name", "Test User")
   155	    git("config", "user.email", "test@example.com")
   156	
   157	    tracked_file = repo_root / "tracked.txt"
   158	    tracked_file.write_text("first\n", encoding="utf-8")
   159	    git("add", "tracked.txt")
   160	    git("commit", "-m", "first")
   161	    parent_ref = git("rev-parse", "--short=7", "HEAD")
   162	
   163	    tracked_file.write_text("second\n", encoding="utf-8")
   164	    git("commit", "-am", "second")
   165	
   166	    result = subprocess.run(
   167	        [
   168	            "bash",
   169	            "-lc",
   170	            'source "$1"; REPO_ROOT="$2"; compute_git_ref',
   171	            "bash",
   172	            str(GIT_REF_SCRIPT),
   173	            str(repo_root),
   174	        ],
   175	        capture_output=True,
   176	        text=True,
   177	        cwd=REPO_ROOT,
   178	    )
   179	
   180	    assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
   181	    assert result.stdout.strip() == parent_ref
   182

   184	def test_signed_package_script_builds_ulfo_dmg_without_staging_ds_store(tmp_path):
   185	    app_bundle = tmp_path / "Plow.app"
   186	    output = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
   187	    fake_log_dir = tmp_path / "fake-logs"
   188	    fake_log_dir.mkdir()
   189	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "fake-bin"
   190	    fake_bin.mkdir()
   191	    _create_minimal_valid_app_bundle(app_bundle)
   192	    _write_fake_release_commands(fake_bin)
   193	
   194	    env = {
   195	        **subprocess.os.environ,
   196	        "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   197	        "FAKE_LOG_DIR": str(fake_log_dir),
   198	        "PLOW_RUNTIME_UPLOAD_SCRIPT": str(fake_bin / "upload-runtime-artifacts.sh"),
   199	        "SPARKLE_BIN_DIR": str(fake_bin),
   200	        # PLO-29: the post-staple verify needs a real hdiutil mount; under
   201	        # stubbed hdiutil it can't actually attach the fake DMG, so skip.
   202	        # The artifact-level guard is exercised by
   203	        # test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_dmg_shipping_volume_icon.
   204	        "PLOW_SKIP_DMG_VERIFY": "1",
   205	    }
   206	
   207	    result = subprocess.run(
   208	        [
   209	            str(SIGNED_PACKAGE_SCRIPT),
   210	            "--app-bundle",
   211	            str(app_bundle),
   212	            "--output",
   213	            str(output),
   214	            "--identity",
   215	            "Developer ID Application: Example (3559PD337Z)",
   216	            "--notary-profile",
   217	            "test-notary",
   218	            "--s3-bucket",
   219	            "test-bucket",
   220	            "--release-prefix",
   221	            "beta",
   222	            "--s3-profile",
   223	            "test-profile",
   224	        ],
   225	        capture_output=True,
   226	        text=True,
   227	        cwd=REPO_ROOT,
   228	        env=env,
   229	    )
   230	
   231	    assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
   232	    assert output.exists()
   233	
   234	    hdiutil_log = (fake_log_dir / "hdiutil.log").read_text()
   235	    assert "create" in hdiutil_log
   236	    assert "-format ULFO" in hdiutil_log
   237	    # PLO-29: DMG is created directly as ULFO; the old UDRW->convert dance
   238	    # only existed to host a kHasCustomIcon FinderInfo write on a mounted
   239	    # volume, which we no longer do.
   240	    assert "-format UDRW" not in hdiutil_log
   241	    assert "convert" not in hdiutil_log
   242	
   243	    staged_dir = fake_log_dir / "captured-srcfolder"
   244	    assert (staged_dir / "Plow.app").is_dir()
   245	    assert (staged_dir / "Applications").is_symlink()
   246	    assert not (staged_dir / ".DS_Store").exists()
   247	    assert (staged_dir / ".background" / "background.tiff").is_file()
   248	    # PLO-29: the mounted volume must show the default macOS volume icon,
   249	    # so the staged srcfolder must not ship a .VolumeIcon.icns.
   250	    assert not (staged_dir / ".VolumeIcon.icns").exists()
   251	    assert not (staged_dir / "Plow-rw.dmg").exists()

   254	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   255	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_dmg_shipping_volume_icon(tmp_path):
   256	    """PLO-29 artifact-level guard. Catches the failure mode that
   257	    ``test_signed_package_script_builds_ulfo_dmg_without_staging_ds_store``
   258	    cannot: a regression that re-attaches the DMG post-``hdiutil create``
   259	    and re-stages a custom volume icon at the final-image stage. We build
   260	    three real DMGs with hdiutil and assert plowd-verify-dmg accepts the
   261	    clean one and rejects each regression shape.
   262	
   263	    plowd-verify-dmg is wired into plowd-beta-package-signed between staple
   264	    and S3 upload, so a rejection here aborts ``just release`` before any
   265	    artifact ships."""
   266	    # Refuse to run if a real Plow volume is already mounted: the script
   267	    # bails on that and our assertions would tag the wrong failure mode.
   268	    info = subprocess.run(
   269	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   270	    )
   271	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   272	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   273	
   274	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   275	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   276	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   277	
   278	    def make_dmg(dmg_path: Path, *, volname: str) -> None:
   279	        subprocess.run(
   280	            [
   281	                "hdiutil", "create",
   282	                "-volname", volname,
   283	                "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   284	                "-ov",
   285	                "-format", "ULFO",
   286	                str(dmg_path),
   287	            ],
   288	            check=True, capture_output=True,
   289	        )
   290	
   291	    def run_verify(dmg_path: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
   292	        return subprocess.run(
   293	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg_path)],
   294	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   295	        )
   296	
   297	    # Happy path: clean Plow DMG with no .VolumeIcon must pass.
   298	    clean_dmg = tmp_path / "clean.dmg"
   299	    make_dmg(clean_dmg, volname="Plow")
   300	    ok = run_verify(clean_dmg)
   301	    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"clean DMG rejected: stdout={ok.stdout!r} stderr={ok.stderr!r}"
   302	
   303	    # Regression #1: someone re-introduces .VolumeIcon.icns at the volume root.
   304	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_text("fake-icns")
   305	    iconed_dmg = tmp_path / "iconed.dmg"
   306	    make_dmg(iconed_dmg, volname="Plow")
   307	    fail = run_verify(iconed_dmg)
   308	    assert fail.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns"
   309	    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in fail.stderr
   310	
   311	    # Regression #2: someone parameterizes -volname to something other than "Plow".
   312	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").unlink()
   313	    misnamed_dmg = tmp_path / "misnamed.dmg"
   314	    make_dmg(misnamed_dmg, volname="NotPlow")
   315	    fail2 = run_verify(misnamed_dmg)
   316	    assert fail2.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG with wrong volume name"
   317	    assert "expected 'Plow'" in fail2.stderr
   318	
   319	
   320	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   321	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_propagates_detach_failure_on_success_path(tmp_path):
   322	    """Round-2: if `hdiutil detach` fails on the success path (e.g. the
   323	    volume is busy), plowd-verify-dmg must exit non-zero. The previous
   324	    `|| true` swallowed the failure and returned 0, leaking /Volumes/Plow,
   325	    which then tripped ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume on the next release
   326	    retry. This test injects an `hdiutil` wrapper whose `detach` always
   327	    fails and asserts the script surfaces it."""
   328	    info = subprocess.run(
   329	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   330	    )
   331	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   332	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   333	
   334	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   335	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   336	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   337	    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
   338	    subprocess.run(
   339	        [
   340	            "hdiutil", "create",
   341	            "-volname", "Plow",
   342	            "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   343	            "-ov",
   344	            "-format", "ULFO",
   345	            str(dmg),
   346	        ],
   347	        check=True, capture_output=True,
   348	    )
   349	
   350	    real_hdiutil = subprocess.run(
   351	        ["which", "hdiutil"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   352	    ).stdout.strip()
   353	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
   354	    fake_bin.mkdir()
   355	    wrapper = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
   356	    wrapper.write_text(
   357	        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
   358	        f'if [[ "$1" == "detach" ]]; then\n'
   359	        f'  echo "fake: detach failure (test injection)" >&2\n'
   360	        f'  exit 16\n'
   361	        f'fi\n'
   362	        f'exec "{real_hdiutil}" "$@"\n'
   363	    )
   364	    wrapper.chmod(0o755)
   365	
   366	    try:
   367	        result = subprocess.run(
   368	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg)],
   369	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   370	            env={
   371	                **subprocess.os.environ,
   372	                "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   373	            },
   374	        )
   375	        assert result.returncode != 0, (
   376	            f"verify-dmg returned 0 despite detach failure; mount leaked.\n"
   377	            f"stdout={result.stdout!r}\nstderr={result.stderr!r}"
   378	        )
   379	        assert "failed to detach" in result.stderr, (
   380	            f"expected 'failed to detach' in stderr, got: {result.stderr!r}"
   381	        )
   382	    finally:
   383	        # Real hdiutil to clean up the leaked mount the wrapper refused to release.
   384	        subprocess.run(
   385	            [real_hdiutil, "detach", "/Volumes/Plow"],
   386	            capture_output=True,
   387	        )
   388	
   389

   442	def test_build_runtime_artifacts_rebuilds_when_manifest_version_bumps_but_tarball_is_stale(tmp_path):
   443	    app_root = tmp_path / "app"
   444	    scripts_dir = app_root / "scripts"
   445	    lib_dir = scripts_dir / "lib"
   446	    vm_dir = app_root / "vm"
   447	    output_dir = vm_dir / "output"
   448	    scripts_dir.mkdir(parents=True)
   449	    lib_dir.mkdir(parents=True)
   450	    output_dir.mkdir(parents=True)
   451	
   452	    (scripts_dir / "build-runtime-artifacts.sh").write_text(
   453	        (REPO_ROOT / "app" / "scripts" / "build-runtime-artifacts.sh").read_text(encoding="utf-8"),
   454	        encoding="utf-8",
   455	    )
   456	    (scripts_dir / "build-runtime-artifacts.sh").chmod(0o755)
   457	    (lib_dir / "git-ref.sh").write_text(
   458	        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\ncompute_git_ref() { printf '%s\\n' same123; }\n",
   459	        encoding="utf-8",
   460	    )
   461	    (lib_dir / "git-ref.sh").chmod(0o755)
   462	
   463	    manifest_path = vm_dir / "manifest.toml"
   464	    manifest_path.write_text(
   465	        textwrap.dedent(
   466	            """
   467	            openclaw_version = "2026.4.22"
   468	            openclaw_artifact = "openclaw-agent-2026.4.21.same123.tar.zst"
   469	            openclaw_sha256 = "old-openclaw"
   470	            openclaw_size = 1
   471	            openclaw_git_ref = "same123"
   472	            camoufox_image_version = "135.0.1-beta.25"
   473	            camoufox_image_artifact = "camoufox-135.0.1-beta.24.same123.tar.zst"
   474	            camoufox_image_sha256 = "old-camoufox"
   475	            camoufox_image_size = 1
   476	            camoufox_image_git_ref = "same123"
   477	            """
   478	        ).strip()
   479	        + "\n",
   480	        encoding="utf-8",
   481	    )
   482	
   483	    stale_openclaw = output_dir / "openclaw-agent-2026.4.21.same123.tar.zst"
   484	    stale_camoufox = output_dir / "camoufox-135.0.1-beta.24.same123.tar.zst"
   485	    stale_openclaw.write_text("stale-openclaw\n", encoding="utf-8")
   486	    stale_camoufox.write_text("stale-camoufox\n", encoding="utf-8")
   487	
   488	    build_log = tmp_path / "build.log"
   489	    _write_fake_runtime_child_builder(
   490	        scripts_dir / "build-agent-image.sh",
   491	        build_log,
   492	        "openclaw",
   493	        "openclaw_artifact",
   494	        "rebuilt-openclaw\n",
   495	    )
   496	    _write_fake_runtime_child_builder(
   497	        scripts_dir / "build-camoufox-image.sh",
   498	        build_log,
   499	        "camoufox",
   500	        "camoufox_image_artifact",
   501	        "rebuilt-camoufox\n",
   502	    )
   503	
   504	    result = subprocess.run(
   505	        [str(scripts_dir / "build-runtime-artifacts.sh")],
   506	        capture_output=True,
   507	        text=True,
   508	        cwd=app_root,
   509	    )
   510	
   511	    assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
   512	    assert build_log.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines() == ["openclaw", "camoufox"]
   513	    assert stale_openclaw.read_text(encoding="utf-8") == "rebuilt-openclaw\n"
   514	    assert stale_camoufox.read_text(encoding="utf-8") == "rebuilt-camoufox\n"

   520	    runtime_root = app_bundle / "Contents" / "Resources" / "runtime"

   228	# Mount a Plow DMG and assert no custom volume icon ships at the root

From 4edb57969ae7e2863b328ba5055e5ce1511e9974 Mon Sep 17 00:00:00 2001
From: Swagat Patel <swagatpatel@users.noreply.github.com>
Date: Thu, 30 Apr 2026 18:20:56 -0700
Subject: [PATCH 1/9] PLO-29: drop custom DMG volume icon
MIME-Version: 1.0
Content-Type: text/plain; charset=UTF-8
Content-Transfer-Encoding: 8bit

Mounted Plow DMGs were showing the app icon, which Sam reported as
indistinguishable from the running app in Finder. Strip the custom
icon so the mounted volume uses the default macOS removable-volume
icon while keeping the volume name "Plow".

- plowd-beta-package-signed: stop staging .VolumeIcon.icns; create the
  ULFO DMG directly instead of going UDRW -> attach -> set
  kHasCustomIcon FinderInfo -> detach -> convert. The dance only
  existed to host the icon flag.
- delete the now-orphaned app/plowd/dmg/volume.icns asset.
- add plowd-verify-dmg + `just app dmg-verify` recipe: mounts a built
  DMG, asserts the volume name is "Plow" and that no .VolumeIcon.icns
  ships at the volume root. Smoke-tested locally on three paths
  (happy / .VolumeIcon present / wrong volname) — all behave.
- test_signed_package_script_builds_ulfo_dmg_without_staging_ds_store:
  pin the new contract (no .VolumeIcon.icns staged, no UDRW/convert).

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.7 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>

    18	default_dmg=".build/Plow.dmg"
    19	
    20	dmg_path=""
    21	case "${1:-}" in
    22	  -h|--help)
    23	    usage
    24	    exit 0
    25	    ;;
    26	  "")
    27	    dmg_path="${repo_root}/${default_dmg}"
    28	    ;;
    29	  -*)
    30	    echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
    31	    usage >&2
    32	    exit 1
    33	    ;;
    34	  *)
    35	    dmg_path="$1"
    36	    if (( $# > 1 )); then
    37	      echo "error: unexpected extra arguments: ${*:2}" >&2
    38	      usage >&2
    39	      exit 1
    40	    fi
    41	    ;;
    42	esac
    43	
    44	if [[ "${dmg_path}" != /* ]]; then
    45	  dmg_path="${repo_root}/${dmg_path}"
    46	fi
    47	
    48	[[ -f "${dmg_path}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG not found: ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
    49	
    50	# Refuse to run when a Plow volume is already mounted: the new mountpoint
    51	# would be "Plow 1" / "Plow 2" / ..., which would mask a real regression in
    52	# the volume-name assertion below.
    53	mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
    54	mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
    55	if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
    56	  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before verifying:" >&2
    57	  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
    58	  exit 1
    59	fi
    60	
    61	mounted_volume=""
    62	cleanup() {
    63	  local rc=$?
    64	  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
    65	    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
    66	      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
    67	      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
    68	      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
    69	      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
    70	        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
    71	        exit 1
    72	      fi
    73	    else
    74	      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
    75	      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    76	    fi
    77	  fi
    78	  exit "${rc}"
    79	}
    80	trap cleanup EXIT
    81	
    82	attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${dmg_path}" -nobrowse -readonly)"
    83	# Real `hdiutil attach` prints one line per partition; the data partition's
    84	# last whitespace-delimited field is the mount point. Other lines (e.g. the
    85	# GUID partition scheme) end in a partition-type token that doesn't start
    86	# with "/". Pick the last line whose final field is an absolute path —
    87	# works for both real hdiutil's multi-line tabular output and a single-line
    88	# stub.
    89	mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | awk '$NF ~ /^\// { last=$NF } END { print last }')"
    90	[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to mount ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
    91	
    92	volume_name="$(basename "${mounted_volume}")"
    93	[[ "${volume_name}" == "Plow" ]] || { echo "error: mounted volume name is '${volume_name}', expected 'Plow'" >&2; exit 1; }
    94	
    95	[[ ! -e "${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns" ]] || {
    96	  echo "error: ${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns exists; PLO-29 regression: DMG ships a custom volume icon" >&2
    97	  exit 1
    98	}
    99	
   100	echo "ok: ${dmg_path} mounts as 'Plow' with no custom volume icon"

     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	#
     3	# Interactively record the Finder window layout for the release DMG.
     4	#
     5	# Why this script exists
     6	# ----------------------
     7	# When the user double-clicks the released .dmg, Finder opens the volume
     8	# in a window with a custom background image, hidden toolbar/sidebar,
     9	# and Plow.app + Applications icons in fixed positions. None of that
    10	# styling can be set programmatically by hdiutil — Finder reads it from
    11	# a .DS_Store at the volume root. We used to set up that .DS_Store with
    12	# AppleScript at packaging time, but that automation was flaky in CI and
    13	# was removed in favor of shipping a pre-recorded .DS_Store checked in
    14	# at app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store. plowd-beta-package-signed ditto's that
    15	# file into the staging dir before hdiutil create. So: edits to the
    16	# install-window appearance must be made by re-running this script and
    17	# committing the resulting .DS_Store.
    18	#
    19	# How it works
    20	# ------------
    21	# 1. Stage the same files plowd-beta-package-signed ships: Plow.app,
    22	#    Applications symlink, .background/background.tiff.
    23	# 2. Create a writable (UDRW) DMG and mount it. Finder pops open the
    24	#    volume window; the user arranges it (View Options for background,
    25	#    icon size, arrangement; drag for icon positions and window size).
    26	# 3. User closes the window (Cmd-W), which prompts Finder to flush
    27	#    .DS_Store, and presses Enter at the script's prompt.
    28	# 4. Eject and re-mount. The eject is what guarantees Finder has
    29	#    written .DS_Store to disk; reading it from a still-mounted volume
    30	#    can return a stale or empty file.
    31	# 5. Copy /Volumes/Plow/.DS_Store -> app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store and
    32	#    detach.
    33	#
    34	# Display-size caveat
    35	# -------------------
    36	# .DS_Store stores the install window's bounds as absolute screen
    37	# coordinates relative to the main display. If you record on a large
    38	# display with the window at (e.g.) 2000,1500, Finder on a small
    39	# laptop will reposition the off-screen window to fit, which loses
    40	# your placement. Record near the top-left of your screen and keep the
    41	# window modest (~680x420 fits every Mac display).
    42	#
    43	# Verifying after recording
    44	# -------------------------
    45	# Before committing, build a release DMG (or stage by hand and run
    46	# hdiutil create -format ULFO with the new .DS_Store ditto'd in) and
    47	# open it to confirm Finder honors the layout. The captured .DS_Store
    48	# should grow noticeably (~6 KB+) when a background picture is set;
    49	# a near-8 KB unchanged size suggests the picture didn't take.
    50	#
    51	# Why a separate script (vs inline in plowd-beta-package-signed)
    52	# --------------------------------------------------------------
    53	# This is a one-off authoring tool with mandatory human-in-Finder
    54	# steps; the release script is unattended CI. Keeping them separate
    55	# makes the release path deterministic (just `ditto` a checked-in
    56	# blob) and lets layout changes go through a normal code review of
    57	# the .DS_Store diff.
    58	set -euo pipefail
    59	
    60	usage() {
    61	  cat <<'EOF'
    62	Usage: plowd-record-dmg-layout [--app <path>]
    63	
    64	Records app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store from an interactive Finder layout
    65	session. Mounts a writable scratch DMG that mirrors the staging
    66	plowd-beta-package-signed ships, drops you into Finder to arrange the
    67	install window, then captures the resulting .DS_Store back into the
    68	repo when you press Enter at the prompt.
    69	
    70	Workflow once mounted at /Volumes/Plow:
    71	  1. View > as Icons (Cmd-1)
    72	  2. View > Hide Toolbar (Opt-Cmd-T)
    73	  3. View > Show View Options (Cmd-J)
    74	       - size/position the window (keep it under ~680x420 and near
    75	         the top-left of your screen so it fits on small displays)
    76	       - drag .background/background.tiff into Background > Picture
    77	         (open a second Finder window, Cmd-Shift-. to show hidden
    78	         files, then drag the .tiff into the well; the file picker
    79	         is unreliable for hidden paths)
    80	       - icon size, text size, arrangement = None
    81	  4. Drag Plow.app and Applications icons into position
    82	  5. Close the volume window (Cmd-W) to flush .DS_Store
    83	  6. Press Enter at this script's prompt to capture
    84	
    85	Options:
    86	  --app <path>   Path to the .app to stage. Defaults to the release
    87	                 build at .build/xcode-derived/Build/Products/Release/
    88	                 Plow.app, falling back to /Applications/Plow.app
    89	                 (which is fine for layout-only iteration since icon
    90	                 positions are recorded by filename).
    91	  -h, --help     Show this message.
    92	EOF
    93	}

   289	    echo "submission id: ${submit_id}" >&2
   290	    xcrun notarytool log "${submit_id}" --keychain-profile "${notary_profile}" || true
   291	  fi
   292	  exit 1
   293	fi
   294	echo "stapling notarization ticket..."
   295	xcrun stapler staple "${output}"
   296	echo "checking local Gatekeeper assessment for the DMG..."
   297	if ! spctl --assess --type open -vv "${output}"; then
   298	  echo "warning: local spctl assessment of the DMG failed; notarization was accepted and the ticket was stapled" >&2
   299	fi
   300	
   301	# PLO-29: verify the final shipping artifact has no custom volume icon and
   302	# that the volume name is "Plow" before it gets uploaded. This is mandatory:
   303	# any path that reaches the upload step has been verified.
   304	echo "verifying final DMG against PLO-29 contract..."
   305	"${repo_root}/app/plowd/scripts/plowd-verify-dmg" "${output}"
   306	
   307	echo "writing checksum..."
   308	shasum -a 256 "${output}" > "${output}.sha256"
   309	
   310	echo "signed distribution image created: ${output}"
   311	echo "sha256 file: ${output}.sha256"
   312	profile_args=()
   313	if [[ -n "${s3_profile}" ]]; then
   314	  profile_args=(--profile "${s3_profile}")
   315	fi
   316	
   317	echo "uploading versioned DMG artifacts to S3..."
   318	aws s3 cp "${output}" "s3://${s3_bucket}/${dmg_key}" ${profile_args[@]+"${profile_args[@]}"}
   319	aws s3 cp "${output}.sha256" "s3://${s3_bucket}/${dmg_sha_key}" ${profile_args[@]+"${profile_args[@]}"}
   320	
   321	echo "uploading Sparkle archives to S3..."
   322	publish_args=(
   323	  --archives-dir "${sparkle_stage_dir}"
   324	  --s3-bucket "${s3_bucket}"
   325	  --appcast-key "${sparkle_appcast_key}"
   326	  --archive-prefix "${sparkle_archive_prefix}"
   327	)
   328	publish_args+=(--profile "${s3_profile}")
   329	"${publish_sparkle_script}" "${publish_args[@]}"
   330

   235	# Mounts a writable scratch DMG with production staging, drops you into
   236	# Finder to arrange it, then captures the resulting .DS_Store into
   237	# app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store. That checked-in .DS_Store is shipped verbatim
   238	# by plowd-beta-package-signed in CI; without re-running this recipe,
   239	# layout changes won't reach users. Use whenever you change
   240	# background.tiff, want to move icons, or need to resize the install
   241	# window.
   242	#
   243	# Workflow: arrange the Finder window, close it with Cmd-W (flushes
   244	# .DS_Store), then press Enter at the script's prompt. Defaults --app
   245	# to the release build, falling back to /Applications/Plow.app. See
   246	# plowd/scripts/plowd-record-dmg-layout for shortcuts and caveats.
   247	#
   248	# Re-record the Finder window layout used by the release DMG.
   249	dmg-record-layout app="":
   250	    @if [[ -n "{{app}}" ]]; then \
   251	      plowd/scripts/plowd-record-dmg-layout --app "{{app}}"; \
   252	    else \
   253	      plowd/scripts/plowd-record-dmg-layout; \

   456	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   457	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_dmg_shipping_volume_icon(tmp_path):
   458	    """PLO-29 artifact-level guard. Catches the failure mode that
   459	    ``test_signed_package_script_stages_release_dmg_contents`` cannot:
   460	    a regression that re-attaches the DMG post-``hdiutil create``
   461	    and re-stages a custom volume icon at the final-image stage. We build
   462	    three real DMGs with hdiutil and assert plowd-verify-dmg accepts the
   463	    clean one and rejects each regression shape.
   464	
   465	    plowd-verify-dmg is wired into plowd-beta-package-signed between staple
   466	    and S3 upload, so a rejection here aborts ``just release`` before any
   467	    artifact ships."""
   468	    # Refuse to run if a real Plow volume is already mounted: the script
   469	    # bails on that and our assertions would tag the wrong failure mode.
   470	    info = subprocess.run(
   471	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   472	    )
   473	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   474	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   475	
   476	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   477	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   478	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   479	
   480	    def make_dmg(dmg_path: Path, *, volname: str) -> None:
   481	        subprocess.run(
   482	            [
   483	                "hdiutil", "create",
   484	                "-volname", volname,
   485	                "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   486	                "-ov",
   487	                "-format", "ULFO",
   488	                str(dmg_path),
   489	            ],
   490	            check=True, capture_output=True,
   491	        )
   492	
   493	    def run_verify(dmg_path: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
   494	        return subprocess.run(
   495	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), str(dmg_path)],
   496	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   497	        )
   498	
   499	    # Happy path: clean Plow DMG with no .VolumeIcon must pass.
   500	    clean_dmg = tmp_path / "clean.dmg"
   501	    make_dmg(clean_dmg, volname="Plow")
   502	    ok = run_verify(clean_dmg)
   503	    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"clean DMG rejected: stdout={ok.stdout!r} stderr={ok.stderr!r}"
   504	
   505	    # Regression #1: someone re-introduces .VolumeIcon.icns at the volume root.
   506	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_text("fake-icns")
   507	    iconed_dmg = tmp_path / "iconed.dmg"
   508	    make_dmg(iconed_dmg, volname="Plow")
   509	    fail = run_verify(iconed_dmg)
   510	    assert fail.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns"
   511	    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in fail.stderr
   512	
   513	    # Regression #2: someone parameterizes -volname to something other than "Plow".
   514	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").unlink()
   515	    misnamed_dmg = tmp_path / "misnamed.dmg"
   516	    make_dmg(misnamed_dmg, volname="NotPlow")
   517	    fail2 = run_verify(misnamed_dmg)
   518	    assert fail2.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG with wrong volume name"
   519	    assert "expected 'Plow'" in fail2.stderr
   520	
   521	
   522	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   523	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_propagates_detach_failure_on_success_path(tmp_path):
   524	    """Round-2: if `hdiutil detach` fails on the success path (e.g. the
   525	    volume is busy), plowd-verify-dmg must exit non-zero. The previous
   526	    `|| true` swallowed the failure and returned 0, leaking /Volumes/Plow,
   527	    which then tripped ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume on the next release
   528	    retry. This test injects an `hdiutil` wrapper whose `detach` always
   529	    fails and asserts the script surfaces it."""
   530	    info = subprocess.run(
   531	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   532	    )
   533	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   534	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   535	
   536	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   537	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   538	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   539	    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
   540	    subprocess.run(
   541	        [
   542	            "hdiutil", "create",
   543	            "-volname", "Plow",
   544	            "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   545	            "-ov",
   546	            "-format", "ULFO",
   547	            str(dmg),
   548	        ],
   549	        check=True, capture_output=True,
   550	    )
   551	
   552	    real_hdiutil = subprocess.run(
   553	        ["which", "hdiutil"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   554	    ).stdout.strip()
   555	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
   556	    fake_bin.mkdir()
   557	    wrapper = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
   558	    wrapper.write_text(
   559	        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
   560	        f'if [[ "$1" == "detach" ]]; then\n'
   561	        f'  echo "fake: detach failure (test injection)" >&2\n'
   562	        f'  exit 16\n'
   563	        f'fi\n'
   564	        f'exec "{real_hdiutil}" "$@"\n'
   565	    )
   566	    wrapper.chmod(0o755)
   567	
   568	    try:
   569	        result = subprocess.run(
   570	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), str(dmg)],
   571	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   572	            env={
   573	                **subprocess.os.environ,
   574	                "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   575	            },
   576	        )
   577	        assert result.returncode != 0, (
   578	            f"verify-dmg returned 0 despite detach failure; mount leaked.\n"
   579	            f"stdout={result.stdout!r}\nstderr={result.stderr!r}"
   580	        )
   581	        assert "failed to detach" in result.stderr, (
   582	            f"expected 'failed to detach' in stderr, got: {result.stderr!r}"
   583	        )
   584	    finally:
   585	        # Real hdiutil to clean up the leaked mount the wrapper refused to release.
   586	        subprocess.run(
   587	            [real_hdiutil, "detach", "/Volumes/Plow"],
   588	            capture_output=True,
   589	        )
   590	
   591	
   592	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   593	# Cross-platform verifier tests. These drive plowd-verify-dmg through a fake
   594	# `hdiutil` that points the verifier at a tmp directory whose contents and
   595	# basename the test controls. They exercise the same accept/reject code path
   596	# the real release run takes — no env-skip, no green skip — so the verifier's
   597	# decision logic is covered on every CI lane (including non-macOS ones that
   598	# can't run real hdiutil at all).
   599	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   600	def _write_verifier_fake_hdiutil(fake_bin: Path, mount_path: Path) -> None:
   601	    """Stub `hdiutil` so plowd-verify-dmg attaches to ``mount_path``.
   602	
   603	    The verifier shells out to `hdiutil info` (mount listing), `hdiutil
   604	    attach` (which prints a tabular line whose final column is the mount
   605	    point) and `hdiutil detach` on cleanup. The stub:
   606	
   607	    - prints nothing for `info` (no /Volumes/Plow already mounted)
   608	    - prints `/dev/disk9s1 Apple_APFS <mount_path>` for `attach`
   609	    - succeeds for `detach`
   610	
   611	    The test pre-stages ``mount_path`` with whatever contents and basename
   612	    it wants the verifier to see.
   613	    """
   614	    fake_bin.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
   615	    hdiutil = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
   616	    hdiutil.write_text(
   617	        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
   618	        "case \"$1\" in\n"
   619	        "  info) exit 0 ;;\n"
   620	        f"  attach) printf '/dev/disk9s1 Apple_APFS %s\\n' '{mount_path}'; exit 0 ;;\n"
   621	        "  detach) exit 0 ;;\n"
   622	        "  *) exit 1 ;;\n"
   623	        "esac\n"
   624	    )
   625	    hdiutil.chmod(0o755)
   626	
   627	
   628	def _run_verifier_with_fake_hdiutil(
   629	    tmp_path: Path,
   630	    *,
   631	    mount_basename: str,
   632	    stage_volume_icon: bool,
   633	) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
   634	    """Stage a fake mount + DMG file, run plowd-verify-dmg, return result."""
   635	    mount_path = tmp_path / "fake-mount" / mount_basename
   636	    mount_path.mkdir(parents=True)
   637	    if stage_volume_icon:
   638	        (mount_path / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_bytes(b"fake-icns")
   639	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
   640	    _write_verifier_fake_hdiutil(fake_bin, mount_path)
   641	    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
   642	    dmg.write_bytes(b"fake-dmg")
   643	    return subprocess.run(
   644	        [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), str(dmg)],
   645	        capture_output=True,
   646	        text=True,
   647	        env={
   648	            **subprocess.os.environ,
   649	            "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   650	        },
   651	    )
   652	
   653	
   654	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_accepts_clean_mount_via_fake_hdiutil(tmp_path):
   655	    """Happy path: mount basename is 'Plow' and no .VolumeIcon.icns at root.
   656	    The verifier must accept and exit 0 — no env skip required."""
   657	    result = _run_verifier_with_fake_hdiutil(
   658	        tmp_path, mount_basename="Plow", stage_volume_icon=False,
   659	    )
   660	    assert result.returncode == 0, (
   661	        f"clean mount rejected: stdout={result.stdout!r} stderr={result.stderr!r}"
   662	    )
   663	    assert "ok:" in result.stdout
   664

   666	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_volume_icon_via_fake_hdiutil(tmp_path):
   667	    """The verifier must reject when .VolumeIcon.icns exists at the mount
   668	    root — that is the PLO-29 regression shape it exists to catch."""
   669	    result = _run_verifier_with_fake_hdiutil(
   670	        tmp_path, mount_basename="Plow", stage_volume_icon=True,
   671	    )

   673	        f"verifier accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns: "
   674	        f"stdout={result.stdout!r} stderr={result.stderr!r}"
   675	    )
   676	    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in result.stderr
   677

   680	    """The verifier must reject when the mounted volume's name is not
   681	    'Plow' — guards against someone parameterizing -volname during build."""
   682	    result = _run_verifier_with_fake_hdiutil(

   692	def test_just_dmg_verify_recipe_is_thin_alias_to_verifier(tmp_path):
   693	    """`just app dmg-verify` is the public no-arg entrypoint; it must be a
   694	    pass-through to plowd-verify-dmg, with no extra flags or wrapping that
   695	    would land it on a different code path than the inline release-script
   696	    call. We assert the recipe body forwards positional args verbatim and
   697	    does not pin a flag like `--dmg`."""
   698	    just_text = (REPO_ROOT / "app" / "justfile").read_text()
   699	    # Pull out the dmg-verify recipe block (header line + indented body).
   700	    match = re.search(
   701	        r"^dmg-verify[^\n]*:\n((?:    [^\n]*\n)+)",
   702	        just_text,
   703	        re.MULTILINE,
   704	    )
   705	    assert match is not None, "dmg-verify recipe not found in app/justfile"
   706	    body = match.group(1)
   707	    assert "plowd-verify-dmg" in body
   708	    # Round-3 collapse: the recipe must not pin --dmg or any other flag —
   709	    # one positional pass-through, same code path as the inline release-
   710	    # script call.
   711	    assert "--dmg" not in body, (
   712	        f"dmg-verify recipe still passes --dmg; should be a positional "
   713	        f"pass-through. Recipe body:\n{body}"
   714	    )

+#!/usr/bin/env bash
+#
+# Interactively record the Finder window layout for the release DMG.
+#
+# Why this script exists
+# ----------------------
+# When the user double-clicks the released .dmg, Finder opens the volume
+# in a window with a custom background image, hidden toolbar/sidebar,
+# and Plow.app + Applications icons in fixed positions. None of that
+# styling can be set programmatically by hdiutil — Finder reads it from
+# a .DS_Store at the volume root. We used to set up that .DS_Store with
+# AppleScript at packaging time, but that automation was flaky in CI and
+# was removed in favor of shipping a pre-recorded .DS_Store checked in
+# at app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store. plowd-beta-package-signed ditto's that
+# file into the staging dir before hdiutil create. So: edits to the
+# install-window appearance must be made by re-running this script and
+# committing the resulting .DS_Store.
+#
+# How it works
+# ------------
+# 1. Stage the same files plowd-beta-package-signed ships: Plow.app,
+#    Applications symlink, .background/background.tiff.
+# 2. Create a writable (UDRW) DMG and mount it. Finder pops open the
+#    volume window; the user arranges it (View Options for background,
+#    icon size, arrangement; drag for icon positions and window size).
+# 3. User closes the window (Cmd-W), which prompts Finder to flush
+#    .DS_Store, and presses Enter at the script's prompt.
+# 4. Eject and re-mount. The eject is what guarantees Finder has
+#    written .DS_Store to disk; reading it from a still-mounted volume
+#    can return a stale or empty file.
+# 5. Copy /Volumes/Plow/.DS_Store -> app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store and
+#    detach.
+#
+# Display-size caveat
+# -------------------
+# .DS_Store stores the install window's bounds as absolute screen
+# coordinates relative to the main display. If you record on a large
+# display with the window at (e.g.) 2000,1500, Finder on a small
+# laptop will reposition the off-screen window to fit, which loses
+# your placement. Record near the top-left of your screen and keep the
+# window modest (~680x420 fits every Mac display).
+#
+# Verifying after recording
+# -------------------------
+# Before committing, build a release DMG (or stage by hand and run
+# hdiutil create -format ULFO with the new .DS_Store ditto'd in) and
+# open it to confirm Finder honors the layout. The captured .DS_Store
+# should grow noticeably (~6 KB+) when a background picture is set;
+# a near-8 KB unchanged size suggests the picture didn't take.
+#
+# Why a separate script (vs inline in plowd-beta-package-signed)
+# --------------------------------------------------------------
+# This is a one-off authoring tool with mandatory human-in-Finder
+# steps; the release script is unattended CI. Keeping them separate
+# makes the release path deterministic (just `ditto` a checked-in
+# blob) and lets layout changes go through a normal code review of
+# the .DS_Store diff.
+set -euo pipefail
+
+usage() {
+  cat <<'EOF'
+Usage: plowd-record-dmg-layout [--app <path>]
+
+Records app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store from an interactive Finder layout
+session. Mounts a writable scratch DMG that mirrors the staging
+plowd-beta-package-signed ships, drops you into Finder to arrange the
+install window, then captures the resulting .DS_Store back into the
+repo when you press Enter at the prompt.
+
+Workflow once mounted at /Volumes/Plow:
+  1. View > as Icons (Cmd-1)
+  2. View > Hide Toolbar (Opt-Cmd-T)
+  3. View > Show View Options (Cmd-J)
+       - size/position the window (keep it under ~680x420 and near
+         the top-left of your screen so it fits on small displays)
+       - drag .background/background.tiff into Background > Picture
+         (open a second Finder window, Cmd-Shift-. to show hidden
+         files, then drag the .tiff into the well; the file picker
+         is unreliable for hidden paths)
+       - icon size, text size, arrangement = None
+  4. Drag Plow.app and Applications icons into position
+  5. Close the volume window (Cmd-W) to flush .DS_Store
+  6. Press Enter at this script's prompt to capture
+
+Options:
+  --app <path>   Path to the .app to stage. Defaults to the release
+                 build at .build/xcode-derived/Build/Products/Release/
+                 Plow.app, falling back to /Applications/Plow.app
+                 (which is fine for layout-only iteration since icon
+                 positions are recorded by filename).
+  -h, --help     Show this message.
+EOF
+}
+
+repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
+app_path=""
+
+while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
+  case "$1" in
+    --app)
+      app_path="${2:-}"
+      shift 2
+      ;;
+    -h|--help)
+      usage
+      exit 0
+      ;;
+    *)
+      echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
+      usage >&2
+      exit 1
+      ;;
+  esac
+done
+
+if [[ -z "${app_path}" ]]; then
+  release_app="${repo_root}/.build/xcode-derived/Build/Products/Release/Plow.app"
+  if [[ -d "${release_app}" ]]; then
+    app_path="${release_app}"
+  elif [[ -d "/Applications/Plow.app" ]]; then
+    app_path="/Applications/Plow.app"
+    echo "note: using /Applications/Plow.app (no release build found)"
+  else
+    echo "error: no Plow.app found; pass --app <path>, run 'just app release', or install via /plow-prod-install" >&2
+    exit 1
+  fi
+fi
+[[ -d "${app_path}" ]] || { echo "error: Plow.app not found at ${app_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+bg_src="${repo_root}/app/plowd/dmg/background.tiff"
+ds_dest="${repo_root}/app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store"
+[[ -f "${bg_src}" ]] || { echo "error: background not found: ${bg_src}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
+if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
+  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before recording:" >&2
+  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
+  exit 1
+fi
+
+work_dir="$(mktemp -d /tmp/plowd-dmg-record.XXXXXX)"
+stage_dir="${work_dir}/stage"
+rw_dmg="${work_dir}/layout.dmg"
+mounted_volume=""
+cleanup() {
+  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
+    hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
+  fi
+  rm -rf "${work_dir}"
+}
+trap cleanup EXIT
+
+mkdir -p "${stage_dir}/.background"
+ditto "${app_path}" "${stage_dir}/Plow.app"
+ditto "${bg_src}" "${stage_dir}/.background/background.tiff"
+ln -s /Applications "${stage_dir}/Applications"
+
+hdiutil create -volname "Plow" -srcfolder "${stage_dir}" -ov -format UDRW "${rw_dmg}" >/dev/null
+attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${rw_dmg}" -readwrite -noverify)"
+mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"
+[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to determine mounted volume for ${rw_dmg}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+cat <<EOF
+
+mounted at ${mounted_volume}
+
+In Finder:
+  - View > as Icons (Cmd-1)
+  - View > Hide Toolbar (Opt-Cmd-T)
+  - View > Show View Options (Cmd-J)
+      * size/position the window
+      * drag .background/background.tiff into Background > Picture
+        (Cmd-Shift-. in the picker shows hidden files)
+      * set icon size, text size, arrangement = None
+  - position Plow.app and Applications icons
+  - close the window (Cmd-W) to flush .DS_Store
+
+EOF
+printf "Press Enter when done... "
+read -r _ </dev/tty
+
+hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null
+mounted_volume=""
+
+attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${rw_dmg}" -readwrite -noverify -noautoopen)"
+mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"
+[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to remount ${rw_dmg}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+[[ -f "${mounted_volume}/.DS_Store" ]] || {
+  echo "error: no .DS_Store in mounted volume — did Finder finalize the layout (Cmd-W)?" >&2
+  exit 1
+}
+
+cp "${mounted_volume}/.DS_Store" "${ds_dest}"
+hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null
+mounted_volume=""
+
+echo
+echo "captured ${ds_dest}"
+git -C "${repo_root}" diff --stat -- "${ds_dest}" 2>/dev/null || true

+#!/usr/bin/env bash
+# Mount a Plow DMG and assert it has no custom volume icon (PLO-29 regression
+# guard) and that the volume name is "Plow". Detaches before exiting.
+set -euo pipefail
+
+usage() {
+  cat <<'EOF'
+Usage: plowd-verify-dmg [<dmg-path>]
+
+Mounts the given DMG, asserts the mounted volume is named "Plow" and has no
+.VolumeIcon.icns at its root, then detaches. With no argument, defaults to
+.build/Plow.dmg relative to the repo root. A relative argument is resolved
+against the repo root.
+EOF
+}
+
+repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
+default_dmg=".build/Plow.dmg"
+
+dmg_path=""
+case "${1:-}" in
+  -h|--help)
+    usage
+    exit 0
+    ;;
+  "")
+    dmg_path="${repo_root}/${default_dmg}"
+    ;;
+  -*)
+    echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
+    usage >&2
+    exit 1
+    ;;
+  *)
+    dmg_path="$1"
+    if (( $# > 1 )); then
+      echo "error: unexpected extra arguments: ${*:2}" >&2
+      usage >&2
+      exit 1
+    fi
+    ;;
+esac
+
+if [[ "${dmg_path}" != /* ]]; then
+  dmg_path="${repo_root}/${dmg_path}"
+fi
+
+[[ -f "${dmg_path}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG not found: ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+# Refuse to run when a Plow volume is already mounted: the new mountpoint
+# would be "Plow 1" / "Plow 2" / ..., which would mask a real regression in
+# the volume-name assertion below.
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
+if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
+  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before verifying:" >&2
+  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
+  exit 1
+fi
+
+mounted_volume=""
+cleanup() {
+  local rc=$?
+  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
+    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
+      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
+      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
+      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
+      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
+        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
+        exit 1
+      fi
+    else
+      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
+      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true

  1035	    is the exact regression #478 shape: site-packages/ is present, all files

  1037	    because importlib.metadata can't find the metadata."""

  1079	def test_stage_runtime_installs_plowd_dist_info():
  1080	    """plowd's `importlib.metadata.version("plowd")` calls need `plowd-*.dist-info/`
  1081	    on sys.path. The rsync of the source tree into `${stage_dir}/plowd` doesn't
  1082	    include metadata, so plowd-stage-runtime must explicitly install plowd into
  1083	    site-packages alongside the external deps so the dist-info is present.
  1084	    Without this, packaged apps die at import with PackageNotFoundError before
  1085	    binding the HTTP port (regression #478)."""
  1086	    stage_script = (
  1087	        REPO_ROOT / "app" / "plowd" / "scripts" / "plowd-stage-runtime"
  1088	    ).read_text(encoding="utf-8")
  1089	
  1090	    # Whitespace-tolerant: pin the unique combination of flags that identifies
  1091	    # the dist-info install (--no-deps + ${project_root}) without locking the
  1092	    # script to a specific line-continuation/indent style.
  1093	    assert re.search(
  1094	        r'uv pip install\b[^\n]*'
  1095	        r'(?:\\\s*\n[^\n]*)*'
  1096	        r'--target\s+"\$\{stage_dir\}/site-packages"'
  1097	        r'[^\n]*(?:\\\s*\n[^\n]*)*'
  1098	        r'--no-deps'
  1099	        r'[^\n]*(?:\\\s*\n[^\n]*)*'
  1100	        r'"\$\{project_root\}"',
  1101	        stage_script,
  1102	    ), (
  1103	        "plowd-stage-runtime must `uv pip install --no-deps` plowd into "
  1104	        "${stage_dir}/site-packages so the daemon's importlib.metadata.version"
  1105	        "('plowd') call resolves"
  1106	    )

  1109	def test_runtime_scripts_require_packaged_plow_cli_plugin():

  1228	def test_release_build_recipe_honors_caller_supplied_signing_identity():
  1229	    """Pin the PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY contract introduced in PR #521.
  1230	
  1231	    The Release build path must:
  1232	      1. Default to ad-hoc *only when* the caller hasn't set
  1233	         PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY — otherwise the install skills can't
  1234	         opt into a real Developer ID cert.
  1235	      2. Re-sign post-packaging using whatever identity is set, not a
  1236	         hardcoded `-`. plowd-package-runtime rsyncs into
  1237	         Contents/Resources after Xcode signs; without the re-sign,
  1238	         team-signed bundles ship with an invalid seal.
  1239	    """
  1240	    app_justfile = (REPO_ROOT / "app" / "justfile").read_text(encoding="utf-8")

  1403	
  1404	
  1405	def copy_tree(src: Path, dest: Path) -> None:
  1406	    if dest.exists():
  1407	        shutil.rmtree(dest)
  1408	    dest.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
  1409	    shutil.copytree(src, dest, symlinks=True)
  1410	
  1411	
  1412	def find_value(flag: str, args: list[str]) -> str:
  1413	    return args[args.index(flag) + 1]
  1414	
  1415	
  1416	with (log_dir / "hdiutil.log").open("a") as fh:

  1420	args = sys.argv[2:]
  1421

  1423	    srcfolder = Path(find_value("-srcfolder", args))
  1424	    output = Path(args[-1])
  1425	    output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

  1430	    copy_tree(srcfolder, image_dir)
  1431	    image_map[str(output)] = str(image_dir)
  1432	    save_map()

  1434	
  1435	if command == "attach":

  1438	    # Mount under FAKE_LOG_DIR (not /Volumes) so it is writable on every CI

  1440	    # filesystem reads. The basename "Plow" is what the verifier asserts on.

     2	# Shared helpers for PlowD scripts.

     5	phoenix_to_abs_path() {
     6	  local path="$1"
     7	  local base_dir="${2:-$(pwd)}"
     8	  if [[ "${path}" = /* ]]; then
     9	    echo "${path}"
    10	  else
    11	    echo "${base_dir}/${path}"
    12	  fi
    13	}
    14	
    15	phoenix_manifest_read_string() {
    16	  local manifest_path="$1"
    17	  local key="$2"
    18	  local line value
    19	  line="$(grep -E "^[[:space:]]*${key}[[:space:]]*=" "${manifest_path}" | tail -n 1 || true)"
    20	  if [[ -z "${line}" ]]; then
    21	    echo "error: missing '${key}' in ${manifest_path}" >&2
    22	    exit 1
    23	  fi
    24	  value="${line#*=}"
    25	  value="$(echo "${value}" | sed -E 's/^[[:space:]]*//; s/[[:space:]]*$//; s/^"//; s/"$//')"
    26	  if [[ -z "${value}" ]]; then
    27	    echo "error: empty '${key}' in ${manifest_path}" >&2
    28	    exit 1
    29	  fi
    30	  echo "${value}"
    31	}
    32	
    33	phoenix_status_json_ready() {
    34	  local node_bin="$1"
    35	  local status_json="${2:-}"
    36	  "${node_bin}" -e '
    37	const raw = process.argv[1] || "";
    38	let payload;
    39	try {
    40	  payload = JSON.parse(raw);
    41	} catch {
    42	  process.stdout.write("0");
    43	  process.exit(0);
    44	}
    45	const gateway = payload && typeof payload.gateway === "object" ? payload.gateway : {};
    46	const isReady =
    47	  String(payload.status || "").toLowerCase() === "ok" &&
    48	  Boolean(gateway.running) &&
    49	  Boolean(gateway.operator_connected);
    50	process.stdout.write(isReady ? "1" : "0");
    51	' "${status_json}"
    52	}

### Finding 1 — low
Broken-Glass Test / Concise Code: could the DMG mount primitives move into `app/plowd/scripts/_lib.sh` now that this PR carries multiple copies? `plowd-verify-dmg` and `plowd-record-dmg-layout` both duplicate the “already mounted `/Volumes/Plow`” probe, while `plowd-beta-package-signed` and `plowd-verify-dmg` duplicate the awk mountpoint parser and `plowd-record-dmg-layout` still uses the old sed parser. A tiny shared `plowd_mounted_plow_volumes` / `plowd_hdiutil_mountpoint` helper would reduce repeated shell parsing without adding conditionals, special cases, or a new abstraction layer beyond the existing `_lib.sh`.

### Finding 2 — nit
Broken-Glass Test / Concise Code: could the `justfile` keep only the recipe summary and let `plowd-record-dmg-layout --help` be the source of truth? The just recipe now repeats the Finder workflow and caveats that are already documented in the script’s header and usage text, so every future layout-flow tweak has two prose surfaces to keep synchronized. The remedy is just deletion of duplicated comments, not new guards or abstractions.
